add_namespace = ww1_germany
add_namespace = ww1_germanrework
add_namespace = ww1_german_reichstag

#German Reichstag/Bundestrat

country_event = {
	id = ww1_german_reichstag.1 #1912 Elections
	title = ww1_german_reichstag.1.t
	desc = ww1_german_reichstag.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_elections_1912
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		GER_1912_predicted_seats_calculations = yes
		GER_apply_predictions = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_german_reichstag.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_the_parliament_seats_will_change_tt
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { reichstag_election_date = 1917 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_german_reichstag.3 #1917 elections
	title = ww1_german_reichstag.1.t
	desc = ww1_german_reichstag.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_elections_1912
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		GER_1912_predicted_seats_calculations = yes
		GER_apply_predictions = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_german_reichstag.3.a	
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_the_parliament_seats_will_change_tt
		hidden_effect = { add_to_variable = { reichstag_election_date = 5 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_german_reichstag.2 #Cancelled Elections due to war
	title = ww1_german_reichstag.2.t
	desc = ww1_german_reichstag.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bethmann_hollweg_war
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	option = {
		name = ww1_german_reichstag.2.a
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

# Germany Invades Nationalist France On Metropolitan France
news_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.76
	title = news.155.t
	desc = news.155.d
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_subject = no
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		any_other_country = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
			has_defensive_war_with = PREV
			any_state = {
				is_owned_by = PREV
				is_on_continent = europe
				is_core_of = PREV
				NOT = { state = 1 }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = ger_has_war_with_nfa }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	picture = GFX_news_event_german_soldiers
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = ger_has_war_with_nfa
		}
	}
	major = yes
	option = {
		name = news.155.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_subject_of = GER
				has_war_with = FRA
				has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = news.155.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_subject_of = FRA
				has_war_with = GER
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
			}
		}
	}
}

# GERMAN-POLISH CUSTOMS WAR - REFUSAL TO IMPORT POLISH GOODS WITHOUT CUSTOMS
###############################################################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.93
	title = ww1_germany.93.t
	desc = ww1_germany.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_worker_protests
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_global_flag = interbellum
		has_country_flag = great_war_loser
		has_government = democratic
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = GER_friedrich_ebert
			}
		}
		POL = {
			is_neighbor_of = GER
			has_war = no
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			owns_state = 85			#Westpreußen
			owns_state = 404			#Danzig
			owns_state = 762			#Kattowitz
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.93.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = german_polish_customs_war
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
		}
		send_embargo = POL
		POL = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.94
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.93.b
		add_war_support = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# GERMAN-POLISH CUSTOMS WAR - POLISH REACTION ON EMBARGO
###############################################################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.94
	title = ww1_germany.94.t
	desc = ww1_germany.94.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.94.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
		}
		# High Dependence on trade with Germany
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = 0.05
		send_embargo = FROM
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.94.b
		FROM = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = POL
				modifier = tgwr_opinion_embargo
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 85
					state = 762
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = DNZ
			}
			DNZ = {
				give_military_access = FROM
			}
		}
		else = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = GER
				relation = docking_rights
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# GERMAN-POLISH CUSTOMS WAR - WAR ENDS
###############################################################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.96
	title = ww1_germany.96.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_germany.96.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = GER_adolf_hitler
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_germany.96.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GER_adolf_hitler
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_global_flag = german_polish_customs_war
		has_opinion_modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GER_adolf_hitler
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				POL = {
					exists = yes
					has_opinion_modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = POL
				}
			}
			has_government = communism
			POL = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			is_subject = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.96.a
		break_embargo = POL
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
		}
		POL = {
			break_embargo = PREV
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = POL
				modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GER_adolf_hitler
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.96.b
		break_embargo = POL
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = tgwr_opinion_german_polish_customs_war
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.97
				days = 10
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = GER_adolf_hitler
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.96.c
		add_stability = -0.07
		add_war_support = 0.07
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = GER_adolf_hitler
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

				target = POL
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# REICHSPRAESIDENT - PAUL VON HINDENBURG
###########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.106
	title = ww1_germany.106.t
	desc = ww1_germany.106.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_country_leader = {
			character = GER_friedrich_ebert
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		date > 1925.5.12
		date < 1934.8.2
		has_country_flag = great_war_loser
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.105.a
		retire_character = GER_friedrich_ebert
		GER_paul_von_hindenburg = {
			set_portraits = {
				civilian = {
					large = "gfx/leaders/GER/GER_paul_von_hindenburg_president.png"
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					ideology = conservatism
					traits = {
						monarchist_president
						political_manipulator
						great_war_hero
					}
				}
			}
			promote_character = conservatism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
						long_name = GER_hindenburg_government
						name = GER_hindenburg_government
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
		}
	}
}

# KAPP-LÜTTWITZ PUTSCH - HOW TO COPE
#######################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.110
	title = ww1_germany.110.t
	desc = ww1_germany.110.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ger_civil_war
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				long_name = GER_national_peoples_party_long
				name = GER_national_peoples_party
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_global_flag = kapp_putsch
			set_country_flag = kapp_putsch
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER_kapp
			GER_wolfgang_kapp = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = civilian_dictatorship
					}
					promote_character = civilian_dictatorship
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = civilian_dictatorship
								traits = { staunch_monarchist }
							}
						}
					}	
				}
			}
			GER_walther_von_luttwitz = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
						traits = {
							fascist_militia_leader
						}
					}
				}
				set_unit_leader_flag = kapp_putsch
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			add_ideas = GER_idea_kapp_illegitimate_government
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = GER_freikorps_party
				name = GER_freikorps_party
			}
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 3
				name = kapp_putsch
			}
			news_event = ww1_germany.130
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.110.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_ideas = strikes_3
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.111
				days = 5
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.110.b
		set_country_flag = kapp_civil_war
		add_ideas = strikes_3
		effect_tooltip = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.2
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 7
				name = kapp_putsch
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.2
				states = all
				states_filter = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SAX
						is_core_of = BAD
						is_core_of = HES
						is_core_of = BRU
						is_core_of = ANH
						is_core_of = WUR
						is_core_of = HAN
						is_core_of = OLD
						#is_core_of = SHL
						is_core_of = MEK
						is_core_of = MEC
						state = 987
						state = 54
						state = 60
						state = 57
						state = 55
						state = 42
						state = 869
						state = 989
						state = 793
						state = 28
					}
				}
				capital = 50
				keep_political_party_members = yes
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = old_guard
						has_trait = old_guard_navy
						has_trait = trait_royalist
						has_trait = trait_royal
						has_trait = harsh_leader
						has_unit_leader_flag = kapp_putsch
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = GER_civil_war
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_ideas = strikes_3
					if = {
						limit = {
							owns_state = 59
						}
						GER = {
							set_province_controller = 6513
							set_province_controller = 11402
							set_province_controller = 11493
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = great_war_loser
				set_country_flag = interbellum
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = GER
				hidden_effect = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 5
						communism = 95
					}
					GER = {
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									state = 873
									state = 42
									state = 1185
								}
							}
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
					set_capital = {
						state = 1185
					}
					set_country_flag = ruhr_uprising
					set_country_flag = great_war_loser
					set_country_flag = interbellum
					set_cosmetic_tag = GER_ruhr_revolt
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = communism
						long_name = GER_communism_council_party
						name = GER_communism_council_party
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "GER_workers_councils"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/GER_workers_councils.png"
						ideology = revolutionary_socialism
						traits = {
							our_right_to_survive
						}
					}
					add_ideas = standing_alone
					#load_focus_tree = {
					#	tree = german_focus
					#	keep_completed = yes
					#}
					#uncomplete_national_focus = {
					#	focus = GER_rise_of_evil
					#	uncomplete_children = yes
					#	refund_political_power = no
					#}
					#complete_national_focus = GER_marxism_on_the_rise
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = GER
						size = 1
						target_organization = 1
						source_organization = 1
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Brigade der Rote Armee"
						template_counter = 69
						division_names_group = GER_GAR_02
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							militia = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						}
					}
					1185 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"I Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
							owner = PREV
							prioritize_location = 6469
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"II Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
							owner = PREV
							prioritize_location = 6469
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"III Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
							owner = PREV
							prioritize_location = 6469
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"IV Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
							owner = PREV
							prioritize_location = 6469
						}
					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = GER
							has_war = yes
						}
						declare_war_on = {
							target = PREV
							type = civil_war
						}
						add_civil_war_target = PREV
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.15
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.07
				}
			}
			news_event = ww1_germany.131
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# KAPP-LÜTTWITZ PUTSCH - EMPIRE STRIKES BACK
###############################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.112
	title = ww1_germany.112.t
	desc = ww1_germany.112.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ger_civil_war
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		has_government = neutrality
		has_country_flag = kapp_putsch
		has_country_flag = kapp_civil_war
		has_war = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 70
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.112.a
		add_ideas = GER_revive_the_kaiserreich
		remove_ideas = GER_idea_kapp_illegitimate_government
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_revive_the_kaiserreich_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			remove_ideas = GER_idea_freikorps
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						HOL = {
							is_subject_of = PREV
							owns_state = 7
						}
						controls_state = 7
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = GER_neutrality_party
					name = GER_neutrality_party
				}
				GER_wilhelm_ii = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = GER_wilhelm_ii_desc
							ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
							traits = {
								anti_democrat
								ww_one_trauma
							}
						}
					}
					promote_character = semi_constitutional_monarchy
				}
				else = {
					HOL = {
						country_event = wtt_germany.3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 10
			name = GER_revive_the_kaiserreich
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.112.b
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		remove_ideas = GER_idea_kapp_illegitimate_government
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = -0.3
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

			country_event = ww1_germany.117
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	# CEDE OCCUPATIONS WITH CONDITIONS
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.116.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = ww1_germany.118
		}

			base = 30
		}
	}
	# REFUSE
	option = {

		FROM = {
			country_event = ww1_germany.120
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = FRA
					is_subject_of = PREV
					NOT = {
						is_neighbor_of = NFA
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

# GERMANY CEDES FRENCH OCCUPATIONS WITH NO CONDIIONS

country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.117
	title = ww1_germany.117.t
	desc = ww1_germany.117.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.117.a
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = FRA
				is_subject_of = GER
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					remove_core_of = PREV
					remove_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = GER
						modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_improved_diplomatic_relations
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = GER
						}
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = PREV
						}
						remove_claim_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# GERMANY CEDES FRENCH OCCUPATIONS WITH CONDIIONS
#######################################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.118
	title = ww1_germany.118.t
	desc = ww1_germany.118.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.118.a
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = FRA
				is_subject_of = GER
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					remove_core_of = PREV
					remove_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = no
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 863
							state = 864
							state = 779
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = GER
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						BEL = {
							is_subject_of = GER
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 865
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = BEL
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ENG = {
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
								is_subject = no
							}
						}
						ENG = {
							set_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							CAN = {
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
								is_subject = no
								has_country_flag = has_british_monarchy
							}
						}
						CAN = {
							set_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_other_country = {
							limit = {
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
								is_major = yes
								is_subject = no
							}
							set_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				GER = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.118.b
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = FRA
				is_subject_of = GER
			}
			PREV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = ww1_germany.119
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_germany.122
	title = ww1_germany.122.t
	desc = ww1_germany.122.d

				}

				always = yes
			}

				#	focus = GER_rise_of_evil

				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = GER

					source_organization = 1

						always = yes
					}
				}

					name = "Brigade der Rote Armee"

					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }

						militia = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"I Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 6469
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"II Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 6469
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"III Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
						owner = PREV
						prioritize_location = 6469
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"IV Brigade\" division_template = \"Brigade der Rote Armee\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.3"
						owner = PREV

		865 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
		6 = {
			owner = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							has_country_flag = great_war_winner
						}
					}
					transfer_state = 29
					transfer_state = 33
					transfer_state = 865
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 29
						state = 33
						state = 865
					}
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.134
				hours = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				34 = { is_owned_or_subject_trigger = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { owns_state = 17 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	
		# We are not taking any
		name = ww1_germany.133.c
		trigger = {
			#you must reward your non-subject ally
			NOT = {
				6 = {
					owner = {
						is_subject = no
						has_country_flag = great_war_winner
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 29
					state = 33
					state = 865
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_or_subject_trigger = yes }
				785 = { owner = { transfer_state = PREV.PREV } }
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 29
						state = 33
						state = 865
					}
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.134
				hours = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

# Death of President Hindenburg
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.146
	title = ww1_germany.146.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_cosmetic_tag = GER_nazi }
		text = ww1_germany.146.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GER_nazi } }
		text = ww1_germany.146.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_hindenburg_death
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		OR = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = GER_paul_von_hindenburg
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GER_paul_von_hindenburg
					ruling_only = no
				}
				has_government = fascism
				has_cosmetic_tag = GER_nazi
			}	
		}
		date > 1934.7.1
		is_GER_a_monarchy = no
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 31 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.146.a
		trigger = { has_cosmetic_tag = GER_nazi }
		retire_character = GER_paul_von_hindenburg
		GER_adolf_hitler = {
			add_country_leader_trait = GER_der_fuhrer
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = GER_social_democratic_party_long
				name = GER_social_democratic_party
			}
			GER_otto_wels = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = social_democracy
					}
				}
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # temporal leader
		name = ww1_germany.146.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GER_nazi } }
		retire_character = GER_paul_von_hindenburg
		GER_heinrich_brunning = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = conservatism
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
						long_name = GER_democratic_party_zentrum_long
						name = GER_democratic_party_zentrum
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
		}
	}
}

							has_war_with = VIN
							has_war_with = LAO
							has_war_with = CAM
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							original_tag = VIN
							original_tag = LAO
							original_tag = CAM
						}
					}
					PREV = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = ROOT
							enemy = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 932
						932 = { is_capital = no }
					}
					932 = { add_core_of = PREV }
					set_capital = { state = 932 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				OR = {
					is_neighbor_of = FROM
					any_other_country = {
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					tag = MAL
					tag = SRW
				}
				has_global_flag = british_civil_war
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				tag = IND
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = french_civil_war
					surrender_progress > 0.25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.153.b
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_hostile_diplomatic_relations
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_hostile_diplomatic_relations
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.154
				hours = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.15
				}
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# FROM refused the German protection under the German East Asia
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.154
	title = ww1_germany.154.t
	desc = ww1_germany.154.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.153.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			FROM = { leave_faction = yes }
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				threat > 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				threat > 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 7
				threat > 0.75
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_war_support > 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 7
				has_war_support > 0.75
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { is_major = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.153.b
		add_political_power = -25
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				ENG = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
				FROM = { tag = MAL } 
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = VIN
						tag = LAO
						tag = CAM
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = ww1_germany.166.t
	desc = ww1_germany.166.desc

			805 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			846 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
	}

				}

		}

			}

				}
			}

				add = 5
				has_subject = ROM
			}

				add = 5
				is_in_faction_with = ROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5

					value > 20
				}
			}

	# transfer to ottoman
	option = {

			TUR = {
				owns_state = 211
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}

			limit = {

# Fate of Belarus
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germany.167
	title = ww1_germany.167.t
	desc = ww1_germany.167.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_peaceful_annexation
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		OR = {
			95 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			204 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			206 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = RUS
			has_war_with = SOV
			country_exists = BLR
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 45 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.167.a
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 5
			name = ww1_germany.167.tt
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BLR
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					state = 913
				}
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
			transfer_state_to = BLR
		}
		puppet = BLR
		hidden_effect = {
			BLR = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					last_election = "1908.11.1"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 23
					fascism = 10
					communism = 5
					neutrality = 62
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = BLR_WHR
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							is_GER_a_monarchy = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { date < 1929.4.20 }
						BLR_genrikh = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
									traits = { german_agent foreign_leader }
								}
							}
						}
						GER = {
							GER_albert_wilhelm_heinrich = {
								set_character_name = BLR_genrikh
								set_nationality = BLR
							}
						}
					}	
					else = {
						BLR_uladzimir = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
								}
							}
						}
						GER = {
							retire_character = GER_albert_wilhelm_heinrich
						}
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						long_name = GER_neutrality_party
						name = GER_neutrality_party
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germany.167.b
		trigger = {
			any_other_country = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				OR = {
					tag = NWA
					owns_state = 210
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BLR
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = {
					NWA = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = NWA
				add_core_of = NWA
				NWA = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							OR = {
								has_cosmetic_tag = NWA_pskov_corps
								has_cosmetic_tag = NWA_north_corps
							}						
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = NWA
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				242 = {
					owner = {
						transfer_state = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}		
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				NWA = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}

#1911 Change to Electoral Law in Grand Duchy of Hesse
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.7
	title = ww1_germanrework.7.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_landstande_of_grand_duchy_of_hesse
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		GER_is_hesse_available_in_bundesrat = yes
		has_elections = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.7.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		if = {
			limit = {check_variable = { GER_influence_in_hesse > 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { GER_influence_in_hesse = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = GER_add_INFLUENCE_to_FEDERAL_STATE_tt
				INFLUENCE = "-1"
				FEDERAL_STATE = GER_bundesrat_hesse_tt
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {check_variable = { GER_extra_influence > 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { GER_extra_influence = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = GER_get_extra_influence_tt
				INFLUENCE = "-1"
			}
		}
		#GER_update_bundesrat_gui = yes
		HES = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Constitutional Crisis
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.33
	title = ww1_germanrework.33.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bethmann_hollweg
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.33.a
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		add_war_support = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			deactivate_advisor = GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = GER_state_secretaries_party
			name = GER_state_secretaries_party
		}
		GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						traits = { GER_hamlet }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = GER_wilhelm_ii
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GER_scorned_army
			days = 365
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.34
				hours = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.34
				hours = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.33.b
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		deactivate_advisor = GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg
		GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg = {
			remove_any_country_role_from_character = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
		activate_advisor = GER_georg_michaelis
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = GER_georg_michaelis_resignation_timer
			days = 105
			value = 1
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GER_aftermath_of_the_zabern_affair
			days = 365
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.34
				hours = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Zabern Affair - News

	id = ww1_germanrework.34
	title = ww1_germanrework.34.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.34.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_zabern_affair
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.34.a
		trigger = {
			has_idea = GER_aftermath_of_the_zabern_affair
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.34.b
		trigger = {
			has_idea = GER_scorned_army
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.34.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = GER_aftermath_of_the_zabern_affair
				has_idea = GER_scorned_army
			}		
		}	
	}
}

#1912 Federal Budget
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.45
	title = ww1_germanrework.45.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = GER_1912_budget_rush_mission
	}
	# todo: why do you get the choice between budgets if you can't pass one of them? Bad game design, find a better way to do this
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.45.a #Liberal Budget
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_budget_warning_tt
		remove_ideas = GER_1907_federal_budget
		unlock_decision_tooltip = GER_1912_liberal_budget_law_reich
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_leftist_law_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_passes_bund
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = GER_1912_liberal_federal_budget
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_fails_bund
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.02
			add_political_power = -20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				set_country_flag = GER_liberal_1912_budget
				set_country_flag = GER_1912_budget
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 500
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.45.b #Conservative Budget
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_budget_warning_tt
		remove_ideas = GER_1907_federal_budget
		unlock_decision_tooltip = GER_1912_conservative_budget_law_reich
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_rightist_law_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_passes_bund
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = GER_1912_conservative_federal_budget
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_fails_bund
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.02
			add_political_power = -20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				set_country_flag = GER_conservative_1912_budget
				set_country_flag = GER_1912_budget
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

#Falk Removed
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.47
	title = ww1_germanrework.47.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.47.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ohl_hindenburg
	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		has_war_with = FRA
		is_great_war_ongoing = yes
		war_length_with = {
			tag = FRA
			months > 24
		}
		has_character = GER_erich_von_falkenhayn
		GER_erich_von_falkenhayn = {
			is_army_chief = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.47.a
		remove_advisor_role = {
			character = GER_erich_von_falkenhayn
			slot = army_chief
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_paul_von_hindenburg
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_erich_ludendorff = {
					is_character_slot = political_advisor
					is_hired_as_advisor = no
				}
			}
			fire_random_advisor_if_no_slots = yes	
			activate_advisor = GER_erich_ludendorff
		}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = GER_civilian_government_vs_ohl
			value = 0.15
			tooltip_side = GER_balance_ohl
		}
	}
}

				limit = { has_focus_tree = german_focus }

					}

					}

					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny"

						add_mio_funds = 700
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

#player get free A7Vs
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.79
	title = ww1_germanrework.79.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_a7v
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		OR = {
			has_tech = basic_heavy_tank_chassis
			has_tech = basic_heavy_tank
		}
		has_country_flag = GER_heeringen_tank_plan
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.79.a
		if = {
			limit  ={
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "A7V" 
				type = heavy_tank_chassis_0
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = tank_medium_howitzer
					turret_type_slot = tank_heavy_fixed_superstructure_turret
					suspension_type_slot = tank_bogie_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_riveted_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
					special_type_slot_1 = side_hulled_canons
					special_type_slot_2 = expanded_hull
				}
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 3
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 3
				}
			} 
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = heavy_tank_chassis
				amount = 20
				producer = GER
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = heavy_tank_equipment_1
					amount = 20
					producer = GER
				}
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_focus_on_armored_production
			days = 720
		}
		
	}
}

	id = ww1_germanrework.93
	title = ww1_germanrework.93.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_rizospastis
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = BUL
		has_war_with = GER
		GER = {
			has_country_flag = GER_influencing_newspaper
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GER_influencing_newspaper_done
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = GER_influencing_newspaper_done
	}
	fire_only_once = no
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.93.a		
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

#Should we sell ships to the Netherlands? 
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.94
	title = ww1_germanrework.94.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.94.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.94.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		GER_steal_netherlands_ships = yes
		add_war_support = 0.03
		HOL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = medium_decrease
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.95
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.94.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = HOL
			}
		}
		#sell 4
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER_send_ship_to_netherlands = yes
		}
		HOL = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.96
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	# option = {
	# 	name = ww1_germanrework.94.c
	# 	#sell 4, and allow more selling
	# 	effect_tooltip = {
	# 		GER_send_ship_to_netherlands_plus = yes
	# 	}
	# }
}

#austro-german military cooperation
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.100
	title = ww1_germanrework.100.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.100.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Gotterdammerung"
				NOT = {
					is_special_project_completed = sp:sp_land_super_heavy_howitzer
				}
			}
			sp:sp_land_super_heavy_howitzer = {
				add_project_progress_ratio = 0.5
			}		
		}
		add_breakthrough_points = {
			specialization = specialization_land
			value = 1
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = GER_propose_joint_military_exercises
			bonus = 1
			category = cat_howitzer
			uses = 1
		}
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = GER_propose_joint_military_exercises
			category = land_doctrine
			cost_reduction = 0.25
		}
	}
}

# A New Colonial Secretary
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.101
	title = ww1_germanrework.101.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_colony
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		# Appoint Solf
		name = ww1_germanrework.101.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_unlock_reformist
		set_country_flag = GER_solf_appointed	
		if = {
			limit = { 
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount < 3
					slots = {
						political_advisor
					}
				}
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_wilhelm_solf
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_wilhelm_solf
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Appoint von Liebert
		name = ww1_germanrework.101.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_unlock_hardline
		set_country_flag = GER_von_liebert_appointed
		if = {
			limit = { 
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount < 3
					slots = {
						political_advisor
					}
				}
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_eduard_von_liebert
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_eduard_von_liebert
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

#usa accept mediation
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.111
	title = ww1_germanrework.111.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.111.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_handshake
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.111.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_stability = 0.02
		#now the entente must agree
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GER
				OR = {
					is_major = yes
					tag = ITA #i love you bb
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id =  ww1_germanrework.112
				days = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#minors got the information, but cant act
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = GER
					is_major = no
				}
				country_event = {
					id =  ww1_germanrework.113
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
		USA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.114
				days = 10
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 400
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_germanrework.114
	title = ww1_germanrework.114.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.114.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_handshake
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.114.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_free_belgium
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_get_congo
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					has_war_with = GER
					has_capitulated = no
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_germanrework.115
					days = 2
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ENG = {
							has_war_with = GER
							has_capitulated = no
						}
					}
					ENG = {
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_germanrework.115
							days = 2
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								has_war_with = GER
								has_capitulated = no
							}
							country_event = {
								id = ww1_germanrework.115
								days = 2
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 400
		}
	}
	# option = {

#France refused!
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.116
	title = ww1_germanrework.116.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.116.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_handshake
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.116.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		#unrestricted submarine warfare
		FRA = {
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					has_war_with = GER
					has_capitulated = no
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_germanrework.117
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ENG = {
							has_war_with = GER
							has_capitulated = no
						}
					}
					ENG = {
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_germanrework.117
							days = 3
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								has_war_with = GER
								has_capitulated = no
							}
							country_event = {
								id = ww1_germanrework.117
								days = 3
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 400
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.116.b
		add_war_support = 0.02

			factor = 2
		}
	}

#bye bye hollweg
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.142
	title = ww1_germanrework.142.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.142.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bethmann_hollweg_war
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.142.a
		deactivate_advisor = GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg
		GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg = {
			remove_any_country_role_from_character = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
		activate_advisor = GER_georg_michaelis
		set_country_flag = OHL_command_dictatorship #it change the name to "Silent Dictatorship"
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_erich_ludendorff = {
					is_character_slot = political_advisor
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				GER_erich_ludendorff = {
					swap_country_leader_traits = {
						remove = GER_scheming_intrigant
						add = GER_silent_dictator
						ideology = stratocracy
					}
				}		
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_trait = {
					character = GER_erich_ludendorff
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = GER_scheming_intrigant
				}
				add_trait = {
					character = GER_erich_ludendorff
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = GER_silent_dictator
				}
			}
		}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = GER_civilian_government_vs_ohl
			value = 0.2
			tooltip_side = GER_balance_ohl
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 400
		}
	}
}

# Cracks in the Iron Ring
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.143
	title = ww1_germanrework.143.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.143.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_blockade
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_great_war_ongoing = yes
		has_capitulated = no
		has_war_with_major = yes
		enemies_naval_strength_ratio < 1.3
		NOT = {
			enemies_naval_strength_ratio < 1
			has_war_with = USA
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = GER_famine
			has_idea = GER_food_shortages
			has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
			has_active_mission = GER_mission_food_shortages_timer
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.143.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_famine
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_famine
				add_idea = GER_food_shortages
			}
			activate_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_mission_famine_timer 
				days = 200 
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = GER_mission_food_shortages_timer
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_mission_food_shortages_timer
				days = 180
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_political_power = 15
	}
}

# Blockade shattered
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.144
	title = ww1_germanrework.144.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.144.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_blockade
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_great_war_ongoing = yes
		has_capitulated = no
		has_war_with_major = yes
		OR = {
			has_idea = GER_famine
			has_idea = GER_food_shortages
		}
		NOT = {
			has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
			has_active_mission = GER_mission_food_shortages_timer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_war_with = USA
			}
			USA = { has_capitulated = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_war_with = ENG
			}
			OR = {
				ENG = { has_capitulated = yes }
				enemies_naval_strength_ratio < 1
			}					
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.144.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_blockade_broken_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = GER_famine
			remove_ideas = GER_food_shortages
		}

		clr_country_flag = GER_1912_budget
		clr_country_flag = GER_liberal_1912_budget
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.172.a
		#kaiser force a konservativ budget and Hollweg retire
		trigger = {
			GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg = {
				is_hired_as_advisor = yes
			}
		}
		deactivate_advisor = GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg
		activate_advisor = GER_georg_michaelis
		add_ideas = GER_1912_conservative_federal_budget
		set_country_flag = GER_conservative_1912_budget_passed_in_reichstag
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.172.a
		#kaiser force a konservativ budget and michaelis retire
		trigger = {
			GER_georg_michaelis = {
				is_hired_as_advisor = yes
			}
		}
		deactivate_advisor = GER_georg_michaelis
		activate_advisor = GER_georg_von_hertling
		add_ideas = GER_1912_conservative_federal_budget
		set_country_flag = GER_conservative_1912_budget_passed_in_reichstag
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.172.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				GER_georg_michaelis = {
					is_hired_as_advisor = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				GER_theobald_von_bethmann_hollweg = {
					is_hired_as_advisor = yes
				}
			}
		}
		#kaiser force a konservativ budget
		add_ideas = GER_1912_conservative_federal_budget
		set_country_flag = GER_conservative_1912_budget_passed_in_reichstag
	}

	id = ww1_germanrework.176
	title = ww1_germanrework.176.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.176.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_wilhelm_ii_abdication
	fire_only_once = yes
	 	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		is_GER_a_monarchy = yes
		has_country_flag = great_war_loser
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = GER_1918_revolution
			has_global_flag = interbellum
		}
		has_character = GER_wilhelm_ii
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.176.a
		GER_wilhelm_von_preussen = {
			set_character_name = GER_wilhelm_iii
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GER_wilhelm_ii
				}
			}
			promote_character = GER_wilhelm_von_preussen		
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_idea = GER_wilhelm_ii
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_wilhelm_ii
				add_idea = GER_wilhelm_iii
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_idea = GER_wilhelm_ii_postwar
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_wilhelm_ii_postwar
				add_idea = GER_wilhelm_iii
			}
		}
		GER_wilhelm_ii = {
			set_nationality = HOL
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
			}
		}
	}
}

#TREATY OF BUCHAREST 1918
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.189
	title = ww1_germanrework.189.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.189.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_megali_conference_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.189.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			white_peace = ROM
			ROM = {
				give_military_access = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = treaty_of_bucharest_1918
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						has_war_with = ROM
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = 155
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROM
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = 155
					}
					ROM = {
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								is_core_of = TRA
							}
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROM = {
						owns_state = 867
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						# has_war_with = ROM
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROM
							is_subject_of = ROM
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = 80
					}
					transfer_state = 867
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_other_country = {
						# has_war_with = ROM
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROM
							is_subject_of = ROM
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = 211
					}
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						# has_war_with = ROM
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROM
							is_subject_of = ROM
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = 211
					}
					ROM = {
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									state = 77
									state = 846
								}
							}
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				ROM = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 77
								state = 846
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROM = {
						owns_state = 805
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 805
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROM = {
						owns_state = 79
					}
					MOL = {
						has_war_with = ROM
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = GER
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = MOL
						is_owned_by = ROM
					}
					transfer_state_to = MOL
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = ROM
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = ROM
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = PREV
							is_core_of = PREV
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = ROM
				}
				white_peace = ROM
			}
			ROM = {
				give_resource_rights = {
					receiver = ROOT
					state = 46
				}
				add_ideas = ROM_idea_german_control
				add_ideas = idea_army_restrictions
				add_ideas = idea_armistice
				set_rule = {
					can_join_factions = no
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				every_state = {
					ROM = {
						delete_unit = {
							state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Divizia de Infanterie"
					disband = no
				}
				load_oob = ROM_1916
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_neighbor_of = MOL
						NOT = { has_war_with = MOL }
					}
					MOL = { give_military_access = PREV }
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = GER
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							OR = {
								tag = AUS
								tag = BUL
								tag = MOL
								tag = SER
								tag = HUN
								tag = TRA
								tag = RUS
							}
						}
					}
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROM
					relation = non_aggression_pact
				}
				set_truce = {
					target = ROM
					days = 100
				}
				ROM = {
					give_military_access = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		#historical: two million tons of romanian grain
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = GER_mission_food_shortages_timer }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_mission_food_shortages_timer
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.189.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
				is_owned_by = ROM
				has_resistance = yes
			}
			add_resistance = 30
			add_compliance = -50
		}
	}
}

# Ludendorff Offensive

news_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.193
	title = ww1_germanrework.193.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.193.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_ludendorff_offensive
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.193.a
		trigger = {

				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.193.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.193.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				tag = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
			}
		}
	}
}

# War Plan
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.194
	title = ww1_germanrework.194.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.194.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_schlieffen_plan
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.194.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_schlieffen_moltke_plan
		}
		GER_schlieffen_moltke_plan_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.194.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GER_schlieffen_moltke_plan
				has_completed_focus = GER_heeringens_plan
			}
		}
		GER_schlieffen_plan_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.194.a
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_heeringens_plan
		}
		GER_heeringens_plan_effect = yes
	}
}

# Belgium refuses ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.195
	title = ww1_germanrework.195.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.195.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.195.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				BEL = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = FRA
					}
				}
				NOT = { 
					has_global_flag = BEL_granted_german_passage
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BEL
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
			add_state_claim = 906 # Arelerland
			add_state_claim = 907 # Ardenne
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = kis_news.130 # Invasion of Belgium
			}
		}

		# Belgian Congo?
		# add_state_claim = 295
		# add_state_claim = 718
		# add_state_claim = 538
	}
}

# Entente doesn't accept violation of Dutch neutrality
country_event = {
	id = ww1_germanrework.199
	title = ww1_germanrework.199.t
	desc = ww1_germanrework.199.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_germanrework.199.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = HOL
		}
		HOL = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = neutrality_idea
				}
				remove_ideas = neutrality_idea
			}
		}		
	}
}
